## Scientific Double Blind Clinical Pilot Study of


## Dr. Frank Ryan’s Abdominal Fat Reducer

Commissioned by Advanced Supplement Research and con­
ducted by a research group which has an expert staff consisting
of more than 32 board-certified physician investigators and more
than 38 ACRP certified clinical research coordinators. This group
conducts clinical studies for the major drug companies.
Test subjects did not exercise or diet differently. Both treatment
groups were provided calorie restricted diet instructions, were given
a daily dosage of Dr. Frank Ryan’s Abdominal Fat Reducer or Placebo.
Dr. Frank Ryan’s Abdominal Fat Reducer group experienced a 400%
reduction in fat mass, 4 times reduction in BMI at 4 weeks, 4 times
greater weight loss at 4 weeks, 2 times reduction in waist circumfer­
ence and nearly a 50% decrease in calorie and carbohydrate intake.
(To review this clinical study, log on to www.clinicalstudiespubitshmg.coni)

n advanced line of prod-

Endless Youth and Life which

than their age.

ducer.

stubborn fat to reduce and it is al-

health. Abdominal fat produces
destructive hormones that spread
throughout the body. A pilot clini-

pot belly.

ACRP certified clinical research

How does Dr. Frank Ryan’s
Abdominal Fat Reducer work?
John Whitehead, spokesperson for
Endless Youth and Life explained.
Whitehead revealed, “It was
found in a number of research
studies on laboratory animals and
later confirmed in human studies,
that a substance called Conjugated
Linoleic Acid (CLA) decreases
abdominal body fat in three ways:
1.) CLA decreases abdominal
body fat mass by decreasing the
amount of abdominal fat that is
stored after eating; 2.) CLA in-
creases the rate of fat breakdown
in abdominal fat cells; and 3.)
CLA increases the rate of abdomi-
nal fat metabolism which decreas-
es the total number of fat cells.
You can think of CLA as a match
that lights the fuse in abdominal
fat. This fuse also increases meta-
bolic rate that can result in more
fat loss. Dr. Frank Ryan’s Abdom-
inal Fat Reducercontains the ef-
fective dose of CLA.
Whitehead said, “There are
also a number of other beneficial
effects to CLA that help decrease
the future storage of fat.”
“CLA interferes with an en-
zyme called lipoprotein lipase
(LPL). LPL is an enzyme that
helps store fat in the body. 2 So,
by inhibiting this fat-storing en-
zyme LPL, CLA can help reduce
the re-accumulation of fat.”
“CLA also helps the body use
its existing abdominal fat for en-
ergy, thereby increasing fat oxi-
dation and energy expenditure.”
Dr. Frank Ryan’s Abdominal
Fat Reducer also contains other
super highly advanced all-natur-

abdominal fat. Of course, a

inal fats. 3, 4, 5 One of these ingre-

potent extract of green tea. This
extract is EGCG, which has been

Scientific Double Blind Clinical Pilot Study of
Dr. Frank Ryan’s Abdominal Fat Reducer
Commissioned by Advanced Supplement Research and
conducted by a research group which has an expert staff
consisting of more than 32 board-certified physician in-
vestigators and more than 38 ACRP certified clinical re-
search coordinators. This group conducts clinical studies
for the major drug companies.
Test subjects did not exercise or diet differently. Both treat-
ment groups were provided calorie restricted diet instructions,
were given a daily dosage of Dr. Frank Ryan’s Abdominal Fat
Reducer or Placebo. Dr. Frank Ryan’s Abdominal Fat Reducer
group experienced a 400% reduction in fat mass, 4 times re-
duction in BMI at 4 weeks, 4 times greater weight loss at 4
weeks, 2 times reduction in waist circumference and nearly a
50% decrease in calorie and carbohydrate intake.
(To review this clinical study, log on to www.clinicalstudiespublishing.com)

M.D.,Ph.D.aformerclinicalprofes-

# Dieters lose weight without adding exercise or diets


# while taking newly-released weight loss discovery


# Pharmacies can’t get new diet pill

## SHOWN IN CLINICAL TRIAL


## How scientists believe new Apatrim ™ works

HYPOTHALAMUS
Apatrim may help suppress the feelings
of hunger sent from the stomach to the
Hypothalamus in the brain*

## Clinical studies show


## how Apatrim works

1. Suppresses appetite*
Apatrim may help suppress the
hunger sensory mechanism
of the hypothalamus.
2. Limits fat accumulation*
Apatrim may hinder the enzyme
Citrate Lyase which helps reduce
fat accumulation in the body.
3. Reduces fat formation*
Apatrim may inhibit the enzyme
Malonyl Coenzyme A which helps
the body in the formation of fat.
NEW APATRIM
Clinical trends suggest it helps inter-
rupt hunger signals so APPETITE IS
SUPPRESSED*
New Apatrim has been clinically tested and scientific trends suggest this
new diet supplement uses multiple mechanisms of action that can assist in
weight loss as illustrated:
By M.J. MOORE
FIGURE 1
Universal Media Syndicate
UMS - Call Center operators are
bracing for the surge of calls from
dieters around the country who will
be trying to get this newly released
diet pill.
This new weight loss supplement,
which is not available in stores, is
every dieter’s dream.
The developers of this remarkable
discovery have named it Apatrim™.
Everyone who has struggled with
weight loss would surely agree;
they would love to lose weight and
inches without changing their diet
or adding exercise to their daily
routine.
Well, that’s exactly what the clini-
cal trial 1 showed and that’s why this
new weight loss supplement is get-
ting so much attention.
Participants in the clinical trial
who took the supplement as directed
got great results and they were in-
structed not to add any exercise or
change eating habits.
Scientists believe that Apatrim
can suppress appetite which may
mean fewer calories being con-
sumed. Consumers should keep in
mind that there is no substitute for
proper diet and exercise when it
comes to losing weight. Meaning-
ful weight loss requires consum-
ing fewer calories than the body
burns.
Apatrim can be taken with com-
plete confidence; there is no danger
of embarrassing side effects.* This
is unlike a recently approved ‘fat
blocking’ diet product where the
potential to experience ‘accidents’
exists.
WHY SO MUCH EXCITEMENT?
Scientists have uncovered an
amazing compound that has a known
ability to naturally control hunger
pangs.*
This compound comes from a
natural plant extract, and is not a
drug. It is the active ingredient in
Apatrim, and has been clinically
shown to get excellent results that
include weight loss and a reduction
in waistline.*¹
A clinical study showed that
participants taking Apatrim’s ac-
tive ingredient lost an average of 5
times more weight than those tak-
ing a placebo. Participants also lost
an average of 1 inch off their waist-
line, with some losing as much as
3 inches in just 4 weeks.*¹
These great results are what’s get-
ting everyone so excited about this
new weight loss breakthrough.
“The initial feedback from every-
one who’s heard about Apatrim has
been incredible, they can’t wait to
start using it,” said Valerie Land,
Director of Call Center Operations.
CLINICAL RESULTS
The U.S. clinical study was con-
ducted in Los Angeles under the
direction of Dr. Ronald M. Lawrence, 2
M.D., Ph.D. a former clinical profes-
sor at the University of California’s
Los Angeles School of Medicine.
The study included healthy, over-
weight individuals between the
ages of 31 and 73. Their caloric in-
take and level of exercise was not
disclosed.
The participants were instructed
not to change the food they were
eating and not to add any exercise;
in other words, no changes to their
daily routine. They were told to take
Apatrim 30 minutes before lunch
and dinner.
The results were stunning.
An amazing 100% of the partici-
pants who took the active ingredi-
ent as instructed either lost weight
or inches off their waistline during
the 4 week study.* In contrast, only
one person taking the placebo lost
weight, just half-a-pound, and not
one reduced their waistline.
Some participants experienced in-
credible results, losing as much as 8
pounds and up to 3 inches off their
waistline.* 1
Apatrim may just be the weight
loss breakthrough that people who
want to lose weight without starv-
ing or suffering through intense
exercise have been waiting for.
And who knows how much weight
people could lose if exercise and a re-
duced calorie diet were added while
taking Apatrim.
HOW IT WORKS
The active ingredient in Apatrim
comes from a plant that grows in
India.
This ‘miracle’ plant is Caralluma
Fimbriata and it has been used
by native tribes in India for centu-
ries to reduce hunger and quench
thirst during times of famine and
drought.*
Until recently, the only way to
get these benefits was to eat the
plant.
But scientists have developed a
proprietary method of extraction
that is protected by U.S. Patent
#7,060,308. This process enables
Apatrim’s manufacturer to put the
plant’s benefits into a pill.
Scientists believe Apatrim’s active
ingredient works by blocking the
hunger signals that are sent from
the stomach to the brain (Figure 1).
The brain then thinks that the stom-
ach is full, causing a reduction in
appetite.*
This can mean less calories being
eaten which everyone knows leads to
weight loss.*
HIGHLY RECOMMENDED
Professionals in the weight loss
industry are recommending Apatrim
to their clients.
Dr. Joseph Dietz, Director of Health
Science, Research & Development for
PatentHEALTH, LLC., the health care
company that developed Apatrim,
was very impressed with the weight
loss and safety data coming from the
clinicals.
“While there is no substitute for
proper diet and exercise, when I saw
the results from the clinical trials, I
immediately recommended that we
use this new compound in Apatrim,”
said Dr. Dietz.
“In addition to these great results,
Apatrim is stimulant free and has no
reported adverse effects.”
“Scientific trends also suggest
that in addition to appetite con-
trol, Apatrim can help block the
enzymes that cause body fat to ac-
cumulate and form,” added Dietz.*
When all the possible benefits
of this weight loss supplement are
considered, it’s no wonder profes-
sionals are recommending it to their
clients.
HOW TO GET IT
Apatrim is now available to diet-
ers in the U.S.; but it is not being sold
in pharmacies. Those that want this
new diet supplement must contact
the company directly.
The company has set up
National Order Hotlines to han-
dle the expected surge of calls
from people who want this
weight loss breakthrough
right now. Consumers must
call the number assigned
to their region and ask for
Dept. AP832. The coun-
try has been divided into
3 regions so everyone
has a fair chance to get
Apatrim.
Initial supplies are
limited and operators
have been instructed
to fill orders on a first-
come, first-served
basis. Those not get-
ting through may have
to wait until more
product is produced,
which could take as
long as six weeks.
Great results, no
embarrassing side
effects and clinically
supported data. It’s
not hard to see why
Apatrim appears to
be the smart choice for
anyone who wants to
lose weight without suf-
fering through intense ex-
ercise or unhealthy diets. (cid:78)

joints,butalsoactsasacomfortable
shockabsorber. 6666
“Synovial fluid is part of what
allows young people to be highly
active without getting sore joints.
But as we age, the body’s natural
production of this fluid declines.
This can force the bones in our
joints to grind together which can
lead to nagging discomfort,” said
Dr.Dietz.

# MAJOR BREAKTHROUGH


# New pill targets fat and water in the


# abdomen that cause the pot belly


# Developed from studies at the Universities


# of Yale, Pittsburgh, UCLA, and California


# You can say good-bye to your pot belly

By John Whitehead, Media Services
A major new breakthrough
pill with ingredients that tar­
get abdominal fat and water
that cause the pot belly has
been announced by BioTech
Research1®.
The brand name of this pill
is AbGONE'* It is now avail­
able to the public.
AbGON E'“ was devel­
oped from concepts in re­
search conducted at the Uni­
versities of Yale. Pittsburgh,
UCLA. and California, It was
found in this research that fat
in the abdomen is different
than the rest of your body.
And. there are 2 types of ab­
dominal fat, outer fat and in­
testinal fat.
Certain factors cause fat to
collect in the abdominal area
in excess.
But what makes abdominal
fat different from the rest of
the fat in the body also provid­
ed researchers with a way to
reduce it with a number of nat­
ural substances which reduce
both types of abdominal fat.
They also found a way to re­
duce excess abdominal water.
The lead developer of this
remarkable new pill, Ab-
GONE'*, with these ingredi­
ents that reduce abdominal fat
and water. was Rehan Jalali,
nationally recognized nutri­
tionist and author for BioTech
Research .
Here is my eye-opening
interview with Mr. Jalali, Re­
seat cli studies are noted and
referenced in this interview *
Q. Mr. .filial!, how did
you develop this remark­
able AbGONE'" pill with in­
gredients that target fat and
water in the abdomen?
A. Ii took live years to de­
velop the AbGONE'* pill,
We started out by review­
ing large volumes of research
that had been done on why so
much fat is disproportionately
stored in the abdomen. This
research was conducted at
Yale University.2
This research found that
abdominal fat was different
than in the rest of the body.'
From this initial research,
we knew we could develop a
pill to reduce abdominal fat.
We also found that there
were harmful effects of ab­
dominal excess fat and excess
retained water. These includ­
ed the fact that people with a
pot hells had a greater ten­
dency to certain health prob-
Ictus.2 We also found that
they had social difficulties
and had greater rates of un­
employment and divorce.'
Q, It has always been
thought in the scientific
community that you could
not spot reduce fat. Is that
not true?
A. I he ingredients in Ab
GONE do not spot reduce or­
dinary fat. They help reduce
ordinary fat uniformly over the
entire body The ingredients in
AbGON I:* enable the body to
reduce excess water and fat in
lite abdomen that the body
could not reduce before And
they help inhibit the excess
collection of abdominal fat iii
AbGONE'” lead developer Rehan
Jalali is a nationally recognized nu­
tritionist and author who has ap­
peared in NEWSWEEK, Muscle & Fit­
ness, Oxygen, Men's Fitness, Mus­
cle Media and many other maga­
zines and scientific journals. He has
developed over IOO cutting edge
products for the nutritional supple-
ment industry._________________

deep in the abdomen.

domen is reduced in size much
better than bebite
O How is abdominal fat
different from other fat in
the body?
A Abdominal tat is much
more sensitive to a certain
hormone which enlarges the
fat. I will elaborate shortly.
There are basically tw o dit-
ferent typesot fat in the body,
The first is outer fat found un­
der the skin surface. The sec-
Now', this is important.
It is possible to reduce the
surface fat in the body but
still have significant abdomi­
nal intestinal fat.
That is why. even when
people become super thin and
have no visible fat on their
body, they often still have a
pot belly. That is because the
intestinal fat is still collected
deep iii the abdomen.
Q. How do the ingredi­
ents in ANGONE1* help re­
duce abdominal surface and
intestinal fat?
A, We found in a number
of research studies on labora­
tory animals, later confirmed
iii human studies, a substance
called Conjugated Linoieic
Acid (CUA). Studies of GLA
suggest that CLA decreases
body fat in three ways: I.)
CLA decreases body fat mass
by decreasing the amount of
fat that is stored after eating;
2.) CLA increases the rate of
fat breakdown in fat cells; and
3.) CLA increases the rate of
fat metabolism which de­
creases the total number of fat
cells. You can think of CLA
as a match that lights the fuse
in fat. This fuse increases the
metabolic rate of fat that can
result in subsequent fat loss.
Studies have shown that
you cun reduce abdominal fat
within 4 weeks. AbGONE'*
contains a good dose of CLA.
There are also a number of
other beneficial effects to
CLA that help decrease the
future storage ot tut

of Tat ?

en/y me called lipoprotein li­
pase

bodylfe. So. by inhibiting this

can help reduce the re accumu­

CLA also helps the body
use its existing fat tor energy,
thereby increasing fat oxida­
tion and energy expenditure.

fects Higher levels ot Corti­
sol arc harmful.

(AP) - Moderate Palestinian

Intensified Hamas rocket
that had collapsed under a

sides reached a truce over the
weekend, but tensions re­

dispute over the security
forces remains unresolved.
In a challenge to that shaky
internal truce, gunmen
opened fire from a passing
car late Wednesday on the

least two of his bodyguards.
fire accompanying the Pales­

Israel would have to be com­
prehensive, and include the
West Bank in addition to
Gaza. The previous truce,
brokered in November, ap­
plied only to the Gaza-Israel
border, and Israel rejected re­
peated Palestinian demands
that it also halt arrest raids in
the West Bank.
The meeting ended with
the two sides agreeing their
factions would meet again.

# House OKs


# stiff penalties


# for gasoline


# price gouging

WASHINGTON (AP) - Re­
sponding to high costs at the
pump, the House approved leg­
islation Wednesday that would
outlaw gasoline price gouging.
• Many lawmakers said that
may be easier to say than to de­
tect or enforce.
The legislation would penalize
individuals or companies for
taking "unfair advantage" or
charging "unconscionably exces­
sive" prices for gasoline and oth­
er fuels.
Opponents said the language
was too vague and that the Fed­
eral Trade Commission, which
would enforce the law, has not
clearly defined price gouging.
"I don't know what 'uncon­
scionably excessive' means,"
said Rep. Joe Barton, R-Texas.
The bill's chief sponsor, Demo­
cratic Rep. Bart Stupak of Michi­
gan, said he had no doubt the
FTC would be able to determine
price gouging once the agency
had a law to uphold.
The measure would establish
the first federal law against en
r
ergy price gouging. The FTC
now can investigate price ma­
nipulation under antitrust laws.
Currently, 29 states have price
gouging statutes; enforcement
varies widely.
Stupak's proposal only would
go into effect - and then for just
30 days - if the president de­
clared an energy emergency.
The bill calls for penalties of
up to $150 million for compa­
nies and up to $2 million and 10
years imprisonment for individ­
uals found to be engaged in
price gouging.
Twenty-nine state have vari­
ous price gouging statutes, but
the vary widely in enforcement
The FTC has investigated alle­
gations of price manipulation
but failed to find widespread vi­
olations. In a report last year, the
agency said an investigation af­
ter Hurricane Katrina hit in
2005 uncovered 15 incidents
that could have been price goug­
ing. But other factors also could
have explained the high prices,
it said.

## Thursday, April 8, 2004 THE GAZETTE METRO 3

PAID ADVERTISEMENT
<02004 Meda Seivlcss S-5542 OF10343R-1

# New pill helps reduce body fat without


# Ephedra, other stimulants or side effects


# Clinical studies show increased energy expenditure


# boost; also brealcs through weiglit loss plateauing


# From studies at Universities of Berkley, Purdue and Ciiicago

By John Whitehead, Madia Senlcas
A new diet pill, UpoGONE™,
has been developed which
contains ingredients that help
reduce body fat without stim-
ulants like Ephedra or bad
side effects.
In fact, LipoGONE™ can
help support overall health.
LipoGONE™ ingredients
also help the body break
through weight loss plateau-
ing that all people experience
after they lose weight for a
number of weeks, then, slow
down or stop.
LipoGONE™ was devel-
oped by BioTech Research
from concepts in research at
the Universities of Berkley,
Purdue and Chicago. One of
the lead developers was Dr.
Karlis Ullis M.D., a weight loss
and anti aging specialist who
services many movie stars and
models in the Hollywood area.
Dr. Ullis was also a faculty
member of The UCLA Med-
ical School for 30 years. He
recently left to devote full
time to his booming practice..
Here is my most enlightening
interview with Dr. Ullis. •Clin-
ical studies referenced.
Q. Dr. Ullis, how does Li-
poGONE™ work?
A. LipoGONE™ contains
all natural ingredients that tar-
get body fat loss in 3 very
unique ways.
One: LipoGONE™ contains
ingredients that help to safely
boost natural thyroid hormone
levels. This also breaks the
plateau wall people hit when
they lose weight. Thyroid hor-
mones control calorie burning,
body temperature regulation
and protein synthesis.
Two: LipoGONE™ contains
ingredients that help regulate
and stabilize blood sugar levels,
' by regulating insulin produced
by the pancreas. Therefore, you
don't have excess fat storage
that occurs when you have very
high levels of blood glucose.
These ingredients also optimize
nutrient absorption into the
muscle tissue so that you can
get nutrients such as amino
acids and glucose into lean
muscle tissue versus converting
them into fat.
Three: LipoGONE™ con-
tains ingredients that help pro-
vide thermonutrients that
boost natural heat production
and metabolism internally to
support the fat loss process. It
helps to substantially increase
the amount of calories a per-
son burns per day. It is done
without harmful stimulants.
LipoGONE™ is a complete
non-stimulant product that has
clinical studies on each ingre-
dient.
Q. How do LipoGONE™
ingredients safely boost thy-
roid hormone levels and
break through weight loss
plateauing?
LipoGONE™ contains in-
gredients called gugguls-
terones. This is an herb that has
been used for thousands of
years in herbal medicine.
Therefore, it is time proven to
be safe. It comes from India.
There is research showing that
it can help normalize thyroid
hormone levels. Studies on
guggulsterones show it can
help reduce triglycerides'''-,
which is another effect of thy-
roid hormones, and it was
shown to increase both T4 and
T3 levels.-"
Here is a little background
on thyroid hormones. The T4
thyroid hormone, or thyroxin,
is an inactive thyroid hormone
and T4 then converts into T3.
You can think of T3 as an ac-
tive thyroid hormone. The T4
¿Ortverts into T3in the livetr-
road block which is called
weight loss plateauing. That is
because your body wants to
maintain homeostasis which
So you have inactive thyroid
hormone that converts to ac-
tive thyroid hormone, which
can then help maintain a
healthy metabolism that caus-
es fat loss to occur,
Guggulipid is another
name for guggulsterones.
Guggulipid has been used to
help normalize thyroid hor-
mone levels because after
long periods of dieting, peo-
ple essentially cannot lose
anymore weight. They hit a
means keeping things as they
are. Over a long period of diet-
ing, your body starts lowering
your natural thyroid hormone
level to keep body fat at the
same level. Therefore, you
cannot lose anymore fat. Gug-
gulipid actually helps normal-
ize those thyroid hormone lev-
els to a normal level that al-
lows you to continue increas-
ing metabolic rate and allow-
ing you to increase fat loss.
There are also bonus bene-
fits. Studies on guggulipid have
shown that it lowers LDL,
which is a "bad" cholesterol,
while increasing HDL, which
is a "good" cholesterol, as an
added effect. It has been used
for many years, and one other
positive effect is that it has
been used to treat acne as well.
Another LipoGONE™ in-
gredient that works along with
guggulipid to normalize thy-
roid hormone levels is a micro
mineral known as selenium.
There's a specific form of sele-
nium in LipoGONE™ called
selenium methionine, which is
a very active highly absorbable
form of this mineral. Selenium
besides having anti-oxidant ef-
fects and regulating blood sug-
ar levels, helps convert inac-
tive thyroid, T4, into T3.
Q. You said 14 and T3
levels decrease in the body
when you are dieting and
cause plateauing. Why?
A. If you're on a low calo-
rie diet, your body wants to
maintain your weight. And
your body has been trained to
hold on to fat. So if you cut
calories for a long period of
time, say for 4 to 6 weeks,
what happens is your body
thinks it is not getting enough
calories, and it wants to hold
on to body fat because of the
famine that might be coming.
The way it does that is it low-
ers both T4 and T3 thyroid
hormone levels.
Q. Thyroid hormones are
a pretty potent thing. Will
this increase thyroid hor-
mone too much?
A. No. Guggulsterone and
selenium actually normalize
thyroid hormone levels, so
they don't boost it to where
you have extremely high lev-
els of thyroid hormone levels.
You eventually normalize it to
the levels that allow you to
continue to lose fat even after
long periods of dieting so you
do not plateau.
Q. How ilo the ingredi-
ents in LipoGONE™ regu-
late blood sugar levels which
helps inhibit excess fat stor-
age?
Your body has a hormone
called insulin. Insulin is kind
of a double-edged sword. It is
used to helped dispose of an
increase in glucose. If you eat
a meal that contains carbohy-
drates, they raise blood sugar,
which is glucose, levels. So,
insulin starts being released
from the pancreas to help dis-
pose of that glucose. The first
thing insulin does is it takes
glucose and other nutrients in-
to the muscle tissue, which is
good,because then you can
stimulate lean body mass.
However, any extra glucose,
which is why a lot of people

# New research finds the 5 causes of the


# abdominal bulge and the quickest,


# easiest ways to flatten it like a board.


# Excess fat is NOT the biggest cause.

By John Whitehead
(Canton, OH) New research has
finally uncovered why the lower
abdomen bulges out and how to cor-
rect this stubborn problem.
There are a multitude of reasons
that the lower abdomen bows out and
why it is so difficult to flatten. Many
of the reasons have nothing to do with
excess fat.
But, now the lower abdomen can
be flattened using little-known, new
advanced methods developed from
this new research by certified personal
trainer Frank Campitelli. These meth-
ods are quick and easy to do right in
your home.
Campitelli' s methods have proven
effective for people with all levels of
fitness and health, from celebrities to
the over forty crowd.
— • Kym Hall is an over forty mother
of two who lost all hope of getting Typical Corrected
back into shape... until she met Frank
Campitelli.
J 1 After five abdominal surgeries and
itwo cesarean births, doctors told Kym
jshe would never have a flat abdomen
;again. When Kym hit the age of forty,
'|he felt very flabby and over weight.
'Her abdomen protruded and her but-
ifocks and arms were sagging and
intoned.
i j After working with Frank for just
•a short while, Kym got results she
'never thought possible. Kym says, "I
jlook better in my forties than I did in
>p\y twenties, thanks to Frank's nieth-
Typical

Myth 1 -I can lose fat by going
on a low-calorie diet only. I don't
need to exercise.
Fact: When you reduce your calo
rie intake without exercising, your
body is designed to perceive that it
will not need muscle in the future, but
rather need fat Therefore, your body
will actually start burning a great deal
of your muscle for energy and actual
ly increase your body fat percentage.
Your metabolic rate (calorie burning
rate) will drop making fat loss very
difficult, extremely slow and likely
impossible.
Myth 2 -All I need to do to lose
fat and shape up is minimal exer
cise such as walking or golf.
Fact: Walking, golfing and other
minimal activities will do next to
nothing to cause you to lose fat
becall~e it bums minimum extrd calo
ries. And you will nol shape up
because it does not adequately stress
the muscles. How many slim and
shapely walkers have you ever seen?
Also, people who think they can get

face ·severe consequences as you will

Myth 3 - I can lose fat and shape
up by eating vegetables and pasta

machines, exei"cise bikes, ski
machines or aerobic classes.
Fact: Aerobic exercise also does
not adequately stress the muscles and
in time will actually lead to flabby
muscles as many long-tin1e aerobic
instructors experience.
The vegetable and pasta diet will
deprive your body of essential protein
needed to maintain muscle mass and
to add the proper muscle needed for
good body shaping. Muscle increases
calorie burning. A pound of muscle
burns 30 calories per day to maintain
while a pound of fat takes nearly zero
calories to 1naintain.
Aerobic exercise is an inefficient
way to lose fat. New university
research has found that anaerobic
exercise (exercise done with resis
tance, mainly weights) burns over
500% more fat than aerobic exercise.
See Figure /. Aerobic exercise stops
burning extra calories when you slop
exercising. Anaerobic exercise, due to
muscle rebuilding, burns many extra
calories long after you stop, even
while you are sleeping. This new
research proves that if you want to
Jose fat slowly, do aerobic exercise.
If you want to lose fat quickly, do
anaerobic exercise.
In addition, aerobic exercise typi
cally bums 25% muscle and 75% fat.
If yOu do extrenie. ainount"> of aerobic
exercise such as long distance run
ning, you will lose weight, but 1nuscJe
too. The muscle loss will make you
will look like a concentration catnp
prisoner, as many marathon runners
look with sunken eyes and skeleton
shapes. Aerobic exercise can be good
for extra cardiovascular benefits if
done in conjunction with anaerobic
exercise.
Anaerobic exercise bums IOOo/o fat
and stresses the muscles. This causes
n1uscle to rebuild and become
stronger. The proceS> of rebuilding
muscle burns a great <1n1ount of extrJ.
calories and, thus, fat. Bodybuilders
jump the amount of ca](lries they bum
per day from 2,5(Xl calorics a day to
over 9,000 calorics per day due to
anaerobic exercise.

# CASE STUDIES

Conducted by Fitness RX in Canton, OH
Studies were conducted for 4 weeks. Some test subjects con
tinued on their own after 4 weeks. There were a total of 19 case
study test subjects. Case study subjects were instructed not to
change their diet or physical activity in any way. Summary re
sults; 89.5% of the subjects reduced their pot belly, waist, hips,
BM! and weight The range of BMI decrease was 2.5 to O with
an average of .9107. The range of inches Jost in the hips was
3.14" to .397" with an average loss of 1.799". The range of
inches lost in the waist was 5" to +.39" with an average of
1.59". The range of weight loss was 2.0 lbs. to 1 lb. with an av
erage weight loss of 7.97 lbs .

# Clinical Trial By Dr. Ronald Lawrence,


# Western Geriatric Research Institute,


# Encino, California


## Active compound was Caralluma Fimbriata extract,


## the active ingredient in Bio SpeedSUM®.

This study was conducted for four weeks. Patients were instructed not to change their
daily activity pattern (exercise), or lheir food intake. They were told not to change their diet
in any way from the preceding four ~eeks before they began laking the substance.

# RESULTS AND SUMMARY

The study was conducted with 26 patients. Nineteen patients were on the active
compound and 7 were on placebo. One patient from each category did not show up for
the final visit Almost every patient taking the active ingredient lost significant weight
Ttrere was almost no weight loss observed in patients on placebo. '
Out of 18 patients, 15 patients (83.33%) Jost weight. Eleven patients (61.11%) lost
about six pounds. The highest loss was nine pounds. Four patients los.t one to two
pounds, and two patients maintained their starting weight. One patient gained 17
pounds. This patient was found nut to complv with the regimen that was requested, and
indeed increased calorii: consumption over the four weeks.

# New gun control restrictions being pushed, but what’s the law?

Gun control in the U.S. is largely governed by a few key federal laws and a variety of state restrictions. The federal government taxes the
making and selling of guns, requires background checks and regulates who can own a gun. Also, states have imposed further restrictions.

The U.S. Constitution
U.S. Supreme Court decisions to overturn handgun
bans in Washington (2008) and Chicago (2010)
affirmed the Second Amendment right to bear arms
applies to individuals.
Federal laws
These major laws are the major federal statutes. A federal assault weapons ban expired in 2004.

1934 National Firearms Act
What it does Imposes a tax on manufacture
and distribution of firearms; requires that
manufacturers and sellers register weapons
with the Justice Department Attorney
General; people who possess an unregis­
tered firearm can be fined up to $250,000 or
sentenced up to 10 years in prison
Background When first passed, the law
was meant to restrict access to firearms
perceived as chosen weapons of
“gangsters," such as machine guns,
short-barreled shotguns and rifles, and
firearm mufflers and silencers; the law was
amended in 1968 to include “destructive
devices,” such as Molotov cocktails and
1968 Gun Control Act
What it does Requires all
commercial manufacturers,
importers or sellers of firearms to be
federally licensed; prohibits sale by
mail across state lines of all
firearms; also specifies categories
of persons who are barred from
possessing firearms, including
felons, fugitives, drug addicts, illegal
immigrants and people who have
been dishonorably discharged from
the armed forces
Background Law details major
federal restrictions in commerce in
small arms and ammunition
1993 Brady Handgun Violence Prevention Act
What it does Requires background checks for all
unlicensed individuals trying to buy a gun from a
federally licensed seller; private transactions subject
to the recordkeeping or background check require­
ments; the law created the National Instant Criminal
Background Check System, designed to determine
one’s elibility to buy a gun; in 1997, the U.S.
Supreme Court ruled that the federal government
cannot force states to participate in the
FBI-administered background check system, this
means some people who should not be allowed to
buy a gun pass through gaps in the database
Background The act, in the name of James Brady,
shot in an attempted assassination of President
Ronald Reagan, amended the Gun Control Act

# The clinically tested way to quiclciy


# lose a pot belly and get firm, flat abs


# The 2 top flat ab products used by Holly­


# wood stars now available to the public

By John Whitehead, Media Services
There is a clinically tested
way to quickly lose your pot
belly and get firm abs as flat as
a board.
There are 2 highly ad­
vanced abdominal flattening
products that were developed
for the Hollywood stars that are
now available to the public.
These 2 advanced products
were developed by a Beverly
Hills Plastic Surgeon and a
Beverly Hills Personal Trainer.
They developed these products
for their clients who included
the most prominent movie
stars, fitness models and pro­
fessional body builders.
What was never before pos­
sible can now be accomplished
with these 2 products to get rid
of abdominal fat and firm and
shape abdominal muscles.
As you may already know,
you can do hundreds of sit-ups
and crunches a day and starve
yourself, but still not lose your
pot belly. There are many rea­
sons for this as was discovered
in scientific studies conducted
by professionals who service
the movie stars, models and
body builders whose living de­
pends on having a flat abdomen.
It was discovered in these
scientific studies that abdomi­
nal fat is different than fat in
the rest of the body.
Abdominal fat is very diffi­
cult to reduce. It is also a very
harmful fat because it produces
bad hormones and other toxic
chemicals that have a destruc­
tive effect on the body. Plus,
there are two types of abdomi­
nal fat: external (subcutaneous
fat) and internal (omental fat)
that is around the intestines.
These scientific studies al­
so found that popular abdomi­
nal exercises such as sit-ups
and crunches in most cases do
not exercise abdominal mus­
cles to a significant degree.
They mainly exercise leg mus­
cles and hip flexor muscles
which are the muscles right
above the legs.
Most people have weak ab­
dominal muscles. Woman who
have babies have especially
weak abdominal muscles. The
weaker the abdominal mus­
cles, the less likelihood they
will be used in doing a sit-up
or crunch. The leg and hip
flexor muscles will do virtual­
ly all of the work. This leaves
the abdominal muscles even
weaker and sagging.
The weak abdominal mus­
cles, especially the lower ab­
dominal muscles which are
thin, are not strong enough to
hold in the intestines. There­
fore, they allow intestinal bulge
which further contributes to the
pot belly. This is why people
who starve themselves to the
point of being anorexic still
have a pot belly.
The 2 advanced abdominal
flattening products that were
developed for the Hollywood
stars provide a 1-2-3 punch to
eliminate the pot belly and
provide firm, flat, shapely ab­
dominal muscles.
This 1-2-3 punch finally re­
duces the three things that
cause the pot belly: 1) excess
external and internal abdominal
fat 2) saggy abdominal muscles
and 3) intestinal bulge.
The 2 products that provide
the 1-2-3 punch are the Dr.
Frank Ryan Abdominal Fat
Reducer and The Grant
Roberts Star ABS™ Machine.
The Dr. Frank Ryan Ab­
dominal Fat Reducer contains
advanced ingredients that re­
duce stubborn abdominal fat
both external and internal.
Dr. Ryan, perhaps the most
famous Hollywood plastic sur­
geon in recent times, was ex­
tensively featured on televi­
sion and in magazines across
the nation.
provided exclusively to the
Hollywood stars.
Dr. Ryan died in a tragic
car accident near his Malibu
ranch in 2010.
However, he made it
known to Endless Youth and
Life that he wished to make
these advance products, which
included his abdominal fat re­
ducer, available to the public.
Endless Youth and Life is
complying with his wishes by
making his products available
to the public starting with his
abdominal fat reducer. Grant
Roberts was a friend of Dr.
Ryan and then also decided to
make his StarABS™ Machine
available to the public along
with Dr. Ryan’s abdominal fat
reducer.
The Grant Roberts
StarABS'“ Machine enables a
person to exercise all the ab­
dominal muscles no matter
how weak they are at the be­
ginning. It also exercises the
deep fiber of the abdominal
muscles never possible before.
There are many abdominal
gimmick exercise machines.
These are flimsy toys that as­
sist with sit-ups and crunches
but still mainly exercise leg
and hip flexor muscles, not ab­
dominal muscles.
A double blind clinical
study was conducted on Dr.
Frank Ryan’s Abdominal Fat
Reducer. The test subjects in
the study lost significant
weight and reduced their pot
belly without changing their
diet or physical activity. Peo­
ple who were not exercising or
dieting lost weight and pot
belly as well as those who
were exercising and dieting.
There are 4 major abdomi­
nal muscle groups: 1 ) Rectus
Abdominus - Front part of
the abs or “The Six-Pack,”
2) Transverse Abdominus -
Deepest muscle of the core and
wraps laterally around abdomi­
nal area. Acts as a natural belt
and keeps your waist tight, 3)
External Obliques - Run diago­
nally on the side of the abs al­
lowing for angled movement
including torso rotation, and 4)
Internal Obliques - Run diago­
nally on the side of the abs al­
lowing for angled movement
including torso rotation. Each
group has 2 muscles for a total
of 8 muscles.
The StarABS'“ Machine is
capable of targeting all 8 ab­
dominal muscles in one effi­
cient machine. Other abdomi­
nal exercises such as sit-ups,
crunches, leg raises and so on
only exercise small parts of
the abdominal muscles.
With The StarABS'“ Ma­
chine you can also concentrate
Dr. Frank Ryan developed a
line of advanced products
along with scientists at Endless
Youth & Life™ that provided
great appearance enhancement
without plastic surgery that he
on various abdominal muscles
by simply adjusting your grip
pressure or leg pressure.
The StarABS™ Machine al­
lows you to adjust the resis­
tance of your abdominal exer­
cise. For beginners the ma­
chine has the unique ability to
actually assist you to complete
the full and proper motion by
simply adding weights to the
“assist” post that enables you
to perform your desired num­
ber of repetitions. As you
progress and your abdominal
core strengthens, you can
gradually add weight to the
opposite “increase resistance”
post to challenge even the
most advanced athlete. There­
fore, you will never outgrow
The StarABS™ Machine and
soon you too will develop
sexy shaped abs like Grant’s
Superstar clients. The regular
price for the StarABS™ Ma­
chine is $472 plus $32 shipping

# New from Biotech Research:


## \$ .


# The fastest, easiest, least ex


# \


# way ever developed to


# slim and muscular at any


# Additional benefits include stronger bones, stronger heart, stronger, thicker and


# more elastic veins and arteries, better mental abilities and increased sex drive

By Frank Campitelli, Certified Personal
Trainer and Nutritionist and Chief of
Research Staff at Biotech Research
(Canton, OH) I wish to. inform you of a new
breakthrough from Biotech Research that has
been proven to bring back youthful appear-
ance and performance in men, virtually turn-
ing the clock back 20 to 30 years.
This new breakthrough is the fastest, eas-
iest and least expensive way ever developed
to make men slim and muscular at any age. It
also produces stronger bones, stronger heart,
arteries and veins and improved body func-
tions including an increased sex drive.
Tests have shown that it can be as much
as 300% faster, reduce the cost by as much
as 96% and put pleasure into losing fat and
saining muscle. You can do it yourself right
in your own home using this scientifically
designed programmed system.
This development also includes the
Biotech Supercompact Full Gym, perhaps
the most compact and least expensive full
gym ever invented. This newly developed
gym, which includes free weights, takes up
only a 4-foot by 4-foot area or 16 square feet
— less than a small couch. Yet it exercises
all muscle groups and builds muscle the
same as a major gym • which would cost over
$40,000.00 and take up 1,500 square feet.
Men who used the method during the
developmental stage reported resulting bene-
fits such as the predictable great increase in
attention and admiration from women due to
their new he-man look. But they also report
other major youthful benefits such as
stronger and more elastic arteries and thicker
bones, stronger heart, stronger and more
elastic arteries and veins and a substantially
increased sex drive.
This method has already worked during
the testing phases for men in their 30's, 40's,
50's and 60"s. I also believe it will work well
for men in their 70 J s or 80's.
One of my clients from the testing phase
is a 55-year old grandfather with 5 grandchil-
dren, Ben Swarey, a CEO of a major compa-
ny. Mr. Swarey says he is now much stronger
and faster after using this system than when
he was in his 20's. In his 20's he was over-
weight, had a pot belly and a 39-inch waist.
With this new method he lost 27 pounds of
fat, gained 12 pounds of muscle, went from
24% body fat to 8% body fat and today has a
body that will rival most men in their 20's.
Also, he now has an abdomen as flat as a
board and a 32-inch waist. He now regularly
competes in baseball, football and basketball
with his grandchildren and many neighbor-
hood children who are in high school.
Before getting into more details about
this methodTl must first tell you about what
does not work to reduce fat, build muscle
and restore youthful body functions. I am
one of the nation's leading experts on fitness.
Concerning my background as an expert,
1 am a certified personal trainer and nutri-
tionist. I have also authored several all-time
best-selling books on nutrition, fat reduction
and body building. My recent hardback best
seller, which you may already know about,
The Campitelli Advanced Method for a Flat
Abdomen and Thin Waist, sold over 150,000
copies in just eleven months. This book was
featured in nearly every newspaper in the
nation.
During my career as a certified personal
trainer and nutritionist and chief of a research
department, I have had to try and test nearly
every method and piece of equipment with
regard to fitness. •
I can save you a great deal of time,
money and grief by telling you about the
popular fitness products that either do not
•work at all or do not work to an adequate
degree. .
"Most of the popular flex-band and row-
ing machines simply are not going to do the
job to build muscle to any adequate degree.
The muscular men used to advertise those
machines did not achieve those bodies using
those machines — that I can assure you.
Those machines do not have the proper resis-
tance through the full cycle of muscle con-
tractions, do not have adequate resistance to
build muscle to a significant degree and they
do not even exercise many critical muscle
groups. The home gyms with weight plates
and a few stations are better but still do not
do the job. They do not exercise enough of
the muscle groups and are limited in move-
ments and weight.
All of those popular skiing action
machines do not provide adequate anaerobic
(muscle-building) exercise and are an unnec-
essary expense for aerobic exercise. You
would do just as well or better for aerobic
exercise with a very inexpensive piece of
equipment I can provide to you.
The aforementioned machines can cost
nearly $1,000.00 for minimal benefit to you.
If you join a health spa or gym with good
equipment, that in itself will not work for
most people because they do not really know
what to do. You need a certified personal
trainer to show you how to exercise properly
to adequately develop an appealing muscular
body. But such spas and gyms represent a
continuing expense. Spas charge upwards of
$30 a month and more, while a personal
trainer charges between $20 to $45 per hour.
You can pay $3,000.00 to over $5,000.00 a
year for a good spa or gym membership with
a personal trainer. But this is also very time-
consuming because of travel time to get there
and many times waiting- to use equipment.
Also, I can testify to you since I have man-
aged health spas and gyms that few'men
stick with their body building programs and
ever accomplish any significant muscle
development because of the expense, incon-
venience and time involved.
Other reasons that few people can
accomplish effective muscle building is that
in the past it has taken too long to develop
significant muscle mass and the routines
were unpleasant and became boring.
We have solved this problem. Our new
system includes the Biotech Supercompact
Full Gym, the most compact full professional,
grade gym ever developed. The heart of a
successful muscle-building program is free
weights. Dumbbells are the most important
free weight, followed by barbells. After this
such things as pull-up bars, pull-down bars
and leg extension apparatus are next in
importance. Any time you see a muscle-
building champion or any man who has
effectively developed their muscles you can
rest assured that free weights and the other
aforementioned items are the heart of their
muscle-development equipment. This gym
contains all of these.
Few people are effective at fat reducing
for the same reasons. The old-style methods
took too long to accomplish fat reduction and
were definitely unpleasant and boring. I will
show you how to get around that problem.
With my advanced nutrition program, I will
show you how to eat more and better-tasting
food than you are now eating and still lose
fat.
We have developed ways to increase
metabolic rate in our clients. We have also
developed advanced muscle-building meth-
ods that drastically cut the time to build mus-
cle mass and make it much more enjoyable.
And we have developed compact
muscle-building equipment for the home that
is very inexpensive but does the same job as
a major gym.
The advanced program that we have
completed from our new developments has
been titled Thg^Campitelli Advanced Method •
Make Men Slim. Muscular And Youthful At
Any Age. My clients have reported the fol-
lowing results and benefits from this pro-
gram:
• A slim and muscular body and the
best appearance, strength, speed and
agility that they have ever had in their
adult life, even including when they
were in their 20's.
• Much more attention and admiration
from women and a much better rela-
tionship with the women in their life.
• Much better health, a reduction of
nagging pains, including a great
reduction in arthritic pain and asthma
attacks and they get sick far less
often. They also report stronger
bones, and better circulation due to a
stronger heart and stronger arteries
and stronger veins.
• Much more energy, greatly improved
mental abilities and mental work
capacity.
• A great boost in confidence.
• A substantial increase in sex drive.
There are many additional benefits to this
program besides fat reduction and muscle
building as indicated by our clients. As you
may have seen in a number of recent news
reports many medical doctors are now call-
ing exercise "the closest thing to- the
Fountain of Youth known to medical sci-
ence."
Lastly, men who exercise, especially
muscle builders enjoy increased sex drive
and better sex. This has been confirmed in a
recent clinical scientific study by physicians
and psychologists at the University of
California at San Diego. The increased sex
drive mainly comes from the increased
testosterone levels produced by muscle
building, and better blood circulation, espe-

# Lose weight without going hungry by


# simply switching your junk food snacks


# to these better tasting Super Food snacks

By: John Whitmore, Media Services
New research at UCLA,
Sam Houston Univ ersity, Penn
State University, Tufts Uni­
versity and many other scien-
tifie institutions have found
substantial evidence to sup
port w hat many experts be­
lieve is the leading cause of
people being overweight and
how to correct it. I
This major cause of ex­
cess weight is not overeating
at the main meals of breakfast,
lunch and dinner. It is snack ­
ing on jiinf food between
meals Bating high protein.
high fiber, nutritious snacks
(Super Food snack si corrects
this problem and produces
substantial weight loss m
many ways.
Finally, you can lose
weight painlessly without go
ing hungry. All you have to do
is switch your junk food
snacks to new ly developed,
better tasting Super Food
snacks.
Endless Youth and Life
Super Food Crackers. Oat­
meal Cookies and Chocolate
Chunk Cookies are high pro­
tein. high antioxidant, good
tiber, low calorie, low
glycerine and low fat, and yet
taste better than lunk food
crackers and cookies.
Super Food snacks help
you lose weight w ithout going
hungry 7 ways:
1) These Super Food
snacks, unlike junk food
snacks, are high in protein.
Protein satisfies hunger much
better and much longer than
carbohydrates and fat, which
make up the majority of the
content of junk food. Super
Food snack customers say just
I ounce of Super Food snacks
satisfies their hunger for 2 to 4
hours. The one ounce sen. tugs
are individually packaged tor
maximum freshness and con­
venience.
2) Super Food snacks con-
tain complex carbohydrates
which are low glycerine. They
take longer to digest and there­
fore do not spike blood sugar.
Junk food is very high in sim­
ple carbohydrates such as
white f lour and sugars w Inch
are high glycemia and spike
blood sugar. This produces a
reaction by the body that
sweeps the excess sugar from
the bloodstream to below nor­
mal levels. This causes you in
minutes to be hungrier than
you were before you started
eating the junk food. Also,
most of the excess blood
sugar is then converted to
stored fat.
3) Junk food is low in
fiber. Super Food snacks con­
tain a good amount of fiber.
Fiber also helps satisfy hunger
and moves food through the
digestive tract faster so that
you are less bloated and your
food in the digestive tract does
not sit and develop toxins.
4) The low protein in junk
food deteriorates your mus­
cles, organs, brain, skin, hair
and nails which are all made
out of protein. Your lean body
mass, mainly muscle, burns
the majority of your calories.
A pound of muscle burns 30
calories per day while a pound
of fat only bums 2 calories per
day. Therefore, every pound
of muscle you lose, you lose
the burning of 30 calories per
day. This means you will keep
storing more and more fat as
you lose more muscle you
lose. You will have to eat less
and less not to gain weight. In
addition, you will look worse
because of unhealthy wrinkled
skin, thin dull hair, and thin
nails that break constantly.
5) High protein snacks are
also important to maintaining
muscles, organs, brain, skin,
hair and nails because protein
has to be in the bloodstream
constantly on demand. The
body cannot store protein
like it stores fat. High protein
snacks are the convenient way
to keep that critical protein in
the bloodstream throughout
the day and even at night.
6) A high protein diet in­
creases the production of good
hormones which increase your
metabolic rate (calorie burning
rate) and assist in the produc­
tion of lean body mass. Protein
also takes many more calories
to digest than carbohydrates
and fat. And, 75% of carbohy­
drates and 100% of fat can be
converted to stored fat. Less
than 30% of protein can be

# After 15 years of failure, man finally discovers the best way to lose weight


# Loses 230 pounds without exercise, pills,


# shakes or counting carbs, calories or fat

a rn m mm ^ ■§ ____ ___ __ Wife loses 23 *85 year old mother loses 51 *friend loses 28
uiT\*nD t: ...i........ i- By JOHN WHITMORE
Media Services
In an amazing new book
called Let's Do Lunch ™
author Roger Troy Wilson
shares the weight loss
secrets he discovered that
allowed him to lose 230
pounds and 24 inches from
his waist without exercising,
without pills, without shakes
and without counting carbs,
calories or fat.
He did it eating carbohy­
drates, protein and fats and
eating until he was com­
pletely full.
His wife, wanting to lose
8 pounds, used his simple
method and quickly lost
23. She looks fabulous.
Roger’s overweight 85-year-
old mother lost the
51 pounds she needed to
lose and a friend, David
Mahmood of Dallas, Texas
(a Type 2 diabetic), not only
lost 28 pounds, but lowered
his blood sugar by 20%.
Roger says, "finally I dis­
covered a way to lose weight
that makes sense. Anyone
can do it because it is so
easy. I want to share it with
every one who is just as frus­
trated as I was try ing to lose
weight.
The popular diets that
you hear about all the time
don't work for most people. /
have tried most or studied
them and I know why.
They severely restrict
what or how much you can
eat which causes terrible
cravings for those foods you
are not suppose to eat. In
some cases they eliminate an
entire category' of foods. It is
impossible to succeed
I've been there. I tried so
many ways to lose weight
that I just wanted to die. I
tried high protein diets, a
liquid diet, measuring and
weighing food and even
acupuncture, to name a few.
I was a diet failure. I just
didn't have the discipline
and will power to succeed.
At one point, for my
daughter's wedding, I was
able to push myself away
from the table for 9 months
and got down to 278pounds.
But the day of the wedding,
even as I was walking her
down the aisle, all I could
think about was pigging-out
at the reception. I gained all
the weight back, and more.
Finally, after 15 years of
trial and error I discovered
how you can lose weight by
actually eating regularfoods
you enjoy and eating until
you are full. And that
includes fats, carbohydrates
and proteins.
There is no need to
prepare special meals; you
and your family can eat
together."
Frankly, after reading his
book for myself and inter­
viewing Roger and Anita, I
was amazed.
Roger calls it a diet. But
when you think of dieting
you think of being hungry.
Craving foods that you
should not be eating. That is
not what Let's Do Lunch 1X1
is about.
He believes in order for a
diet to actually work for the
rest of your life:
A. You must be able to
eat until you are full, only
foods you love and eat
whenever you are hungry.
B. You don't have to eat
foods you don’t like.
C. You have to be able to
satisfy your cravings.
Let's Do Lunch1 M does
all this and more. It is so
easy you cannot fail.
In Lets Do
Roger reveals....
Lunch IAI
The absolute dumbest
thing we all do that keeps us
from losing weight. You
won't believe it! This one
simple change in the way
you eat will help you lose
weight.
What foods you can
eat to eliminate cravings for
foods you should not be
eating.
Which foods he discov­
ered are better for weight
loss when eaten at dinner­
time, which are better eaten
at lunch and which foods lire
better when eaten by them­
selves.
Which foods you proba­
bly think are non-fattening
he found to actually be fat­
tening.
Which foods you proba­
bly think are fattening he
discovered are actually non­
fattening.
Simple ways to mix fat­
tening foods with non-fat­
tening foods to make great
tasting meals that even
children w ill love.
Where to go and what to
get when you want some­
thing quick.
A grocery shopping list
that has the exact foods and
brand names he eats, which
allowed him to achieve his
amazing weight loss.
He even includes 68 spe­
cial recipes you can use if
you like.

weight, my wife Anita could-

cise. She actually thought
there was something wrong
with me. She thought I had a
serious illness.

grace. Anita actually asked

not been able to lose all of

I spent too many years of my life like this!

# Clinical studies find that most overweight people


# are lacking in these 8 fat burning nutrients


# Tablets now available that provide all 8 fat burning nutrients

RESEARCH SUBJECT BSPS-374
He tore After 11 weeks
Research Subject Comments: My name is Lora Ladson, age 41, moth­
er of one. I started Biogenesis and 8 w eeks later, at my son's wedding, peo­
ple couldn't believe it was me. I had gone from a size 12 to a size 8. The
nutrition in Biogenesis really buras fat fast. Now I wear a size 5/6, have
lost a total of 21-5/4 inches and 29 lbs. I can now eat a lot noire food with­
out gaining weight. Unlike other weight loss methods my body now is
shaped, tight and toned. My husband can't stop looking at me and telling
me how wonderful I hmk and how proud he is of me.
By John Whitehead,
Media Services
(Canton, OH) Do you feel that
you do not eat that much food hut
still gain weight for some other
unknown reason? New research
has now found it is not your
imagination.
Clinical studies have found
that many overweight people
lack the proper nutrients to bum
fat efficiently. These studies were
cited in major medical journals
including The American Journal
of Clinical Nutrition, The
International Journal of
Biochemistry, The New England
Journal of Medicine, Current
Therapeutic Research and The
International Journal of Obesity.
A major company, Biotech
Research, also did studies on test
groups of people, some of which
are pictured here.
These studies found that most
overweight people do not take in
any more calories than those peo­
ple who are not overweight. It
was found that most overweight
people can be deficient in the fol­
lowing 8 nutrients that enable the
body to burn fat: L-carnitine,
chromium picolinate, choline,
inositol, biotin, pancreatin
enzyme, betaine enzyme and vit­
amin Bb. These nutrients are
only found in certain foods and
you must get enough of these
nutrients to properly bum fat.
After their studies, Biotech
Research also has recently devel­
oped tablets you can take that
provide all 8 of these critical fat-
burning nutrients.
To make energy from fat there
are numerous chemical pathways
and stages that fat is taken
through (see Figure I). In many
of these stages key nutrients are
needed as catalysts to break
down fat into different compo­
nents. These catalysts and chem­
ical signals include the critical
nutrients choline, inositol, biotin,
and vitamin Bb. Two critic;#!
enzymes are also needed to break
down fat, which are pancreatin
and betaine. Fat also needs to be
transported to the fat burning
chamber of the cell called the
mitochondria. Once outside the
mitochondria, fat is transported
inside with the aid of L-carnitine
and is converted to energy that
the cell can use for other process­
es the cell uses for life. Some of
the other critical nutrients, such
as chromium picolinate, help reg­
ulate and produce insulin; and
insulin helps control hunger, reg­
ulates fat storage, and aids mus­
cle building. These nutrients get
used up in the process. Lack of
these nutrients slows down fat
metabolism. If we supplement
our diet or eat the right foods that
contain these critical nutrients,
our fat metabolism w ill occur at a
very high rate all the time.
There have been numerous
clinical studies that show that
these 8 key nutrients cause peo­
ple to burn fat efficiently, lose
stored fat, and maintain proper
weight. In one of these clinical
studies, reported in the medical
journal Current Therapeutic
Research (51-261-274), a group
of 30 obese women and IO obese
men were placed on diets. The
women were put on a 1200 calo­
rie a day diet and the men a 1600
calorie a day diet. The group was
then split in half. One group was
provided with the adequate
amount of only 2 of the 8 critical
fat burning nutrients, chromium
picolinate and L-carnitine. The
other group was provided with a
placebo pill of inactive ingredi­
ents. The group that was provid­
ed with the fat burning nutrients
lost 15 pounds on average while
the other group lost zero pounds.
New research has also found
that it is not the total amount of
calories taken in per day that
determines weight loss or weight
their calories per day and change
the combinations of the types of
food calorie sources as men­
tioned.
If you lower your calorie
intake dramatically, even going
to I JKK) calories or less a day,
your body will go into survival
mode. It will then shut down
your metabolism and thus firing
fat burning to a very low level. It
will also start breaking down
gain, but rather the food source of
your muscles and internal organs
